+                self.obs_scales.z_pos,
+                self.obs_scales.waist_yrp,
+                self.obs_scales.waist_yrp,
+                self.obs_scales.waist_yrp,
+            ],
+            device=self.device,
+            requires_grad=False,
+        )
+
+        self.amp_obs_joint_indices = []
+        for i in range(self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim):
+            if self.dof_names[i] not in self.cfg.env.amp_obs_ignore_joints:
+                self.amp_obs_joint_indices.append(i)
+
+        print(f'body_names: {self.body_names}')
+        print(f'dof_names: {self.dof_names}')
+        print(f'amp_obs_indices: {self.amp_obs_joint_indices}')
+
+        self.amp_loader = R01AMPLoaderFilter(
+            motion_dataset=self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dataset,
+            motion_dataset_version=self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dataset_version,
+            motion_file_names=self.cfg.env.amp_motion_file_names,
+            preload_transitions=True,
+            device=self.device,
+            time_between_frames=self.dt,
+            num_preload_transitions=self.cfg.env.amp_num_preload_transitions,
+            amp_obs_joint_indices=self.amp_obs_joint_indices,
+        )
+
+        self.torque_deque = torch.zeros(
+            self.torque_deque_size, self.num_envs, self.num_dofs, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device
+        )
+
+        self.rand_leg_linear_dof_pos_offset = torch.zeros(
+            self.num_envs, self.num_dofs, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device
+        )
+
+        # self.base_vel_history = torch.zeros(
+        #     self.num_envs, self.cfg.commands.average_stack, 3, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device
+        # )
+        # self.base_vel_history_sizes = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, dtype=torch.int32, device=self.device)
+        # self.base_avg_vel = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, 3, device=self.device)
+
+        self.actions_teleop = torch.zeros(
+            self.num_envs, self.num_dofs - self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim, device=self.device, requires_grad=False
+        )
+
+        self.sim_step_counter = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, dtype=torch.int32, device=self.device)
+
+        # arm pos command generator for each env
+        self.arm_pos_command_generators = RandomSinSignalGenerator(
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_rand_pos_range] * self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float32, device=self.device
+            ),
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_frequency_range] * self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float32, device=self.device
+            ),
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_phase_range] * self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float32, device=self.device
+            ),
+            self.device,
+        )
+
+        self.arm_pos_command_generators_in_walk = RandomSinSignalGenerator(
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_rand_pos_range] * self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float32, device=self.device
+            ),
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_frequency_range_in_walk] * self.num_envs,
+                dtype=torch.float32,
+                device=self.device,
+            ),
+            torch.tensor(
+                [self.cfg.domain_rand.arm_phase_range] * self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float32, device=self.device
+            ),
+            self.device,
+        )
+
+        self.base_vel_history = torch.zeros(
+            self.num_envs, self.cfg.commands.v_average_stack, 3, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device
+        )
+        self.base_vel_history_size = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, dtype=torch.int32, device=self.device)
+        self.base_avg_vel = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, 3, device=self.device)
+
+        self.z_pos_history = torch.zeros(
+            self.num_envs, self.cfg.commands.z_average_stack, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device
+        )
+        self.z_pos_history_size = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, dtype=torch.int32, device=self.device)
+        self.avg_z_pos = torch.zeros(self.num_envs, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device)
+
+        self.reset_idx(torch.tensor(range(self.num_envs), device=self.device))
+        self.noise_scale_vec = self.get_noise_scale_vec(self.cfg)
+        self.compute_observations()
+
+        self.standing_dof_pos = torch.zeros(self.num_dof, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device, requires_grad=False)
+
+        for i in range(self.num_dofs):
+            name = self.dof_names[i]
+            self.standing_dof_pos[i] = self.cfg.init_state.standing_joint_angles[name]
+
+        self.standing_dof_pos = self.standing_dof_pos.unsqueeze(0)
+
+        self.waist_soft_limit = torch.tensor(
+            self.cfg.rewards.waist_soft_limit, dtype=torch.float, device=self.device, requires_grad=False
+        )
+
+    def get_noise_scale_vec(self, cfg):
+        """Sets a vector used to scale the noise added to the observations.
+            [NOTE]: Must be adapted when changing the observations structure
+
+        Args:
+            cfg (Dict): Environment config file
+
+        Returns:
+            [torch.Tensor]: Vector of scales used to multiply a uniform distribution in [-1, 1]
+        """
+        noise_vec = torch.zeros(self.cfg.env.num_single_obs, device=self.device)
+        self.add_noise = self.cfg.noise.add_noise
+        noise_scales = self.cfg.noise.noise_scales
+        noise_level = self.cfg.noise.noise_level
+
+        commands_noise_idx_s = 0
+        commands_noise_idx_e = commands_noise_idx_s + 7
+        dof_pos_noise_idx_s = commands_noise_idx_e
+
+        dof_pos_noise_idx_e = dof_pos_noise_idx_s + self.amp_loader.joint_pos_dim
+        dof_vel_noise_idx_s = dof_pos_noise_idx_e
+        dof_vel_noise_idx_e = dof_vel_noise_idx_s + self.amp_loader.joint_vel_dim
+        actions_noise_idx_s = dof_vel_noise_idx_e
+        actions_noise_idx_e = (
+            actions_noise_idx_s + self.cfg.env.num_actions + (self.num_dofs - self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim)
+        )
+        pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_s = actions_noise_idx_e
+        pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_e = pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_s + 3
+        pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_s = pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_e
+        pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_e = pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_s + 3
+
+        torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_s = pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_e
+        torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_e = torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_s + 3
+        torso_gravity_noise_idx_s = torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_e
+        torso_gravity_noise_idx_e = torso_gravity_noise_idx_s + 3
+
+        noise_vec[commands_noise_idx_s:commands_noise_idx_e] = 0.0  # commands
+        noise_vec[dof_pos_noise_idx_s:dof_pos_noise_idx_e] = (
+            noise_scales.dof_pos * self.obs_scales.dof_pos * noise_level
+        )
+        noise_vec[dof_vel_noise_idx_s:dof_vel_noise_idx_e] = (
+            noise_scales.dof_vel * self.obs_scales.dof_vel * noise_level
+        )
+        noise_vec[actions_noise_idx_s:actions_noise_idx_e] = 0.0  # previous actions
+
+        noise_vec[pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_s:pelvis_ang_vel_noise_idx_e] = (
+            noise_scales.ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel * noise_level
+        )  # ang vel
+        noise_vec[pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_s:pelvis_gravity_noise_idx_e] = (
+            noise_scales.gravity * noise_level
+        )  # euler x,y
+
+        noise_vec[torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_s:torso_ang_vel_noise_idx_e] = (
+            noise_scales.ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel * noise_level
+        )  # ang vel
+        noise_vec[torso_gravity_noise_idx_s:torso_gravity_noise_idx_e] = noise_scales.gravity * noise_level  # euler x,y
+        return noise_vec
+
+    # def step(self, actions, extra_actions=None):
+    #     """Perform a simulation step with the given actions."""
+    #     obs_buf, privileged_obs_buf, rew_buf, reset_buf, extras = super().step(actions, extra_actions)
+    #     return obs_buf, privileged_obs_buf, rew_buf, reset_buf, extras, self.reset_env_ids, self.terminal_amp_states
+
+    def compute_observations(self):
+        """Compute the observations."""
+
+        if not self.super_init:
+            return
+
+        self.command_input = torch.cat((self.commands[:, :3], self.commands[:, 4:]), dim=1) * self.commands_scale
+
+        q = (self.dof_pos - self.default_dof_pos) * self.obs_scales.dof_pos
+        dq = self.dof_vel * self.obs_scales.dof_vel
+
+        if self.cfg.domain_rand.leg_linear_dof_pos_offset:
+            q += self.rand_leg_linear_dof_pos_offset * self.obs_scales.dof_pos
+
+        privileged_obs_buf = torch.cat(
+            (
+                self.command_input,  # 7
+                (self.dof_pos - self.default_joint_pd_target) * self.obs_scales.dof_pos,  # 23
+                self.dof_vel * self.obs_scales.dof_vel,  # 23
+                self.actions,  # 15
+                self.actions_teleop,  # 8
+                self.base_lin_vel * self.obs_scales.lin_vel,  # 3
+                self.base_ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel,  # 3
+                self.projected_gravity,  # 3
+                self.torso_ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel,  # 3
+                self.torso_projected_gravity,  # 3
+                self.root_states[:, 2].unsqueeze(1),  # 1
+                self.feet_pos,  # 6
+                self.feet_vel,  # 6
+                self.rand_push_force[:, :2],  # 2
+                self.rand_push_torque[:, :],  # 3
+                # self.rand_push_joint_torques[:, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim],
+                self.contact_forces[:, self.feet_indices, 2] / 1000,  # 2
+                # self.rigid_state[:, self.feet_indices, 2] * 2, # 2
+                # self.rigid_state[:, self.feet_indices, 7:10].reshape(self.num_envs, -1),
+            ),
+            dim=-1,
+        )
+
+        random_coef = torch.cat(
+            (
+                self.friction_coeffs_coef.unsqueeze(1),  # 1
+                self.restitutions_coef.unsqueeze(1),  # 1
+                self.payloads_coef.unsqueeze(1),  # 1
+                self.com_displacements_coef,  # 3
+                self.motor_strengths_coef[:, : self.num_actions],  # 15
+                self.Kp_factors_coef[:, : self.num_actions],  # 15
+                self.Kd_factors_coef[:, : self.num_actions],  # 15
+            ),
+            dim=-1,
+        )
+
+        obs_buf = torch.cat(
+            (
+                self.command_input,  # 7 = vel_x, vel_y, aug_vel_yaw, z_pos, waist_yaw, waist_roll, waist_pitch
+                q,  # 23
+                dq,  # 23
+                self.actions,  # 15
+                self.actions_teleop,  # 8
+                self.base_ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel,  # 3
+                self.projected_gravity,  # 3
+                self.torso_ang_vel * self.obs_scales.ang_vel,  # 3
+                self.torso_projected_gravity,  # 3
+            ),
+            dim=-1,
+        )
+
+        if self.add_noise:
+            obs_now = obs_buf.clone() + torch.randn_like(obs_buf) * self.noise_scale_vec
+        else:
+            obs_now = obs_buf.clone()
+        self.obs_history.append(obs_now)
+        self.privileged_obs_history.append(privileged_obs_buf)
+
+        obs_buf_all = torch.stack([self.obs_history[i] for i in range(self.obs_history.maxlen)], dim=1)  # N,T,K
+        self.obs_buf = obs_buf_all.reshape(self.num_envs, -1)  # N, T*K
+
+        privileged_obs_history_stack = torch.cat(
+            [self.privileged_obs_history[i] for i in range(self.cfg.env.c_frame_stack)], dim=1
+        )
+        self.privileged_obs_buf = torch.cat((privileged_obs_history_stack, random_coef), dim=-1)
+        # self.privileged_obs_buf = privileged_obs_history_stack
+
+    # def _compute_torques(self, actions, extra_actions=None):
+    #     """Compute torques from actions.
+    #         Actions can be interpreted as position or velocity targets given to a PD controller, or directly as scaled torques.
+    #         [NOTE]: torques must have the same dimension as the number of DOFs, even if some DOFs are not actuated.
+
+    #     Args:
+    #         actions (torch.Tensor): Actions
+
+    #     Returns:
+    #         [torch.Tensor]: Torques sent to the simulation
+    #     """
+    #     self.actions_teleop = extra_actions
+    #     t = self.sim_step_counter * self.sim_params.dt
+    #     self.actions_teleop = (
+    #         self.arm_pos_command_generators.get_signal(t, self.env_ids).squeeze(-1)
+    #         if extra_actions is None
+    #         else extra_actions
+    #     )
+
+    #     actions_all = torch.cat((actions * self.cfg.control.action_scale, self.actions_teleop), dim=1)
+
+    #     p_gains = self.p_gains * self.Kp_factors
+    #     d_gains = self.d_gains * self.Kd_factors
+    #     p_torques = p_gains * (actions_all + self.default_dof_pos - self.dof_pos)
+    #     p_torques_teleop = p_gains * (actions_all - self.dof_pos)
+
+    #     if self.cfg.domain_rand.torque_delay:
+    #         self.torque_deque[:] = torch.cat([p_torques.unsqueeze(0), self.torque_deque[:-1]], dim=0)
+    #         p_torques = self.torque_deque[self.rand_torque_delay, self.env_ids]
+
+    #     # fill the p torques for direct PD controlled joints
+    #     p_torques[:, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :] = p_torques_teleop[:, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :]
+
+    #     d_torques = -d_gains * self.dof_vel
+
+    #     torques = p_torques + d_torques
+
+    #     torques = torch.clip(torques, -self.torque_limits, self.torque_limits)
+
+    #     # clear push torques for direct PD controlled joints
+    #     for i in range(self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim, self.rand_push_joint_torques.shape[1]):
+    #         self.rand_push_joint_torques[:, i] = 0.0
+
+    #     self.sim_step_counter[:] += 1
+
+    #     return torques * self.motor_strengths
+
+    def _compute_torques(self, actions):
+        t = self.sim_step_counter * self.sim_params.dt
+        self.actions_teleop = self.arm_pos_command_generators.get_signal(t, self.env_ids).squeeze(-1)
+
+        actions_all = torch.cat((actions * self.cfg.control.action_scale, self.actions_teleop), dim=1)
+
+        p_gains = self.p_gains * self.Kp_factors
+        d_gains = self.d_gains * self.Kd_factors
+        p_torques = p_gains * (actions_all + self.default_dof_pos - self.dof_pos)
+        p_torques_teleop = p_gains * (actions_all - self.dof_pos)
+
+        if self.cfg.domain_rand.torque_delay:
+            self.torque_deque[:] = torch.cat([p_torques.unsqueeze(0), self.torque_deque[:-1]], dim=0)
+            p_torques = self.torque_deque[self.rand_torque_delay, self.env_ids]
+
+        # fill the p torques for direct PD controlled joints
+        p_torques[:, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :] = p_torques_teleop[:, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :]
+
+        d_torques = -d_gains * self.dof_vel
+
+        torques = p_torques + d_torques
+
+        torques = torch.clip(torques, -self.torque_limits, self.torque_limits)
+
+        # clear push torques for direct PD controlled joints
+        # for i in range(self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim, self.rand_push_joint_torques.shape[1]):
+        #     self.rand_push_joint_torques[:, i] = 0.0
+
+        self.sim_step_counter[:] += 1
+
+        return torques * self.motor_strengths
+
+    def _post_physics_step_callback(self):
+        super()._post_physics_step_callback()
+
+        vel_set = torch.cat(
+            (self.base_lin_vel[:, :2], self.base_ang_vel[:, [2]]), dim=1
+        )  # [lin_vel_x, lin_vel_y, ang_vel_yaw]
+        self.base_vel_history = torch.cat((vel_set.unsqueeze(1), self.base_vel_history[:, :-1, :]), dim=1)
+        self.base_vel_history_size = torch.clamp(self.base_vel_history_size + 1, max=self.cfg.commands.v_average_stack)
+        self.base_avg_vel = torch.sum(self.base_vel_history, dim=1) / self.base_vel_history_size.unsqueeze(1)
+
+        self.z_pos_history = torch.cat((self.root_states[:, 2].unsqueeze(1), self.z_pos_history[:, :-1]), dim=1)
+        self.z_pos_history_size = torch.clamp(self.z_pos_history_size + 1, max=self.cfg.commands.z_average_stack)
+        self.avg_z_pos = torch.sum(self.z_pos_history, dim=1) / self.z_pos_history_size
+
+    def reset_idx(self, env_ids):
+        """Reset some environments.
+            Calls self._reset_dofs(env_ids), self._reset_root_states(env_ids), and self._resample_commands(env_ids)
+            [Optional] calls self._update_terrain_curriculum(env_ids), self.update_command_curriculum(env_ids) and
+            Logs episode info
+            Resets some buffers
+
+        Args:
+            env_ids (list[int]): List of environment ids which must be reset
+        """
+        if not self.super_init:
+            return
+
+        self.reset_env_ids = env_ids
+        self.terminal_amp_states = self.get_amp_observations()[env_ids]
+
+        # send timeout info to the algorithm every step, even when no envs reset,
+        # to avoid stale time_out values causing wrong V(s) bootstrapping in GAE.
+        if self.cfg.env.send_timeouts:
+            self.extras["time_outs"] = self.time_out_buf
+
+        if len(env_ids) == 0:
+            return
+        # update curriculum
+        if self.cfg.terrain.curriculum:
+            self._update_terrain_curriculum(env_ids)
+        # avoid updating command curriculum at each step since the maximum command is common to all envs
+        if self.cfg.commands.curriculum and (self.common_step_counter % self.max_episode_length == 0):
+            self.update_command_curriculum(env_ids)
+
+        # reset robot states
+
+        if self.cfg.env.play_mode:
+            self.reset_dofs(env_ids, self.default_dof_pos, torch.zeros_like(self.default_dof_pos))
+            self.reset_root_states(
+                env_ids,
+                self.base_init_state[:3].expand(len(env_ids), -1),
+                self.base_init_state[3:7].expand(len(env_ids), -1),
+                self.base_init_state[7:10].expand(len(env_ids), -1),
+                self.base_init_state[10:13].expand(len(env_ids), -1),
+            )
+        else:
+            if self.cfg.env.reference_state_initialization:
+                frames = self.amp_loader.get_full_frame_batch(len(env_ids))
+                self._reset_dofs_amp(env_ids, frames)
+                self._reset_root_states_amp(env_ids, frames)
+            else:
+                self._reset_dofs(env_ids)
+                self._reset_root_states(env_ids)
+
+        self.base_quat[env_ids] = self.root_states[env_ids, 3:7]
+        self.base_euler_xyz = get_euler_xyz_tensor(self.base_quat)
+
+        self._resample_commands(env_ids)
+
+        self._randomize_dof_props(env_ids)
+
+        # reset buffers
+        self.feet_pos[env_ids], self.feet_vel[env_ids] = self.r01_kin.foot_states_in_base_frame(
+            self.dof_pos[env_ids, : self.leg_joint_dim].contiguous(),
+            self.dof_vel[env_ids, : self.leg_joint_dim].contiguous(),
+        )
+        self.actions[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.last_actions[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.last_rigid_state[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.last_dof_vel[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.feet_air_time[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.episode_length_buf[env_ids] = 0
+        self.reset_buf[env_ids] = 1
+        # fill extras
+        self.extras["episode"] = {}
+        for key in self.episode_sums.keys():
+            self.extras["episode"]['rew_' + key] = (
+                torch.mean(self.episode_sums[key][env_ids]) / self.max_episode_length_s
+            )
+            self.episode_sums[key][env_ids] = 0.0
+        # log additional curriculum info
+        if self.cfg.terrain.mesh_type == "trimesh":
+            self.extras["episode"]["terrain_level"] = torch.mean(self.terrain_levels.float())
+        if self.cfg.commands.curriculum:
+            self.extras["episode"]["max_command_x"] = self.command_ranges["lin_vel_x"][1]
+        # fix reset gravity bug
+        self.projected_gravity[env_ids] = quat_rotate_inverse(self.base_quat[env_ids], self.gravity_vec[env_ids])
+        torso_quat_in_pelvis = self.r01_kin.torso_rotation_in_pelvis_frame(
+            self.dof_pos[env_ids, self.leg_joint_dim : self.leg_joint_dim + self.waist_joint_dim].contiguous()
+        )
+        self.torso_quat[env_ids] = quat_mul(self.base_quat[env_ids], torso_quat_in_pelvis)
+        self.torso_projected_gravity[env_ids] = quat_rotate_inverse(self.torso_quat[env_ids], self.gravity_vec[env_ids])
+
+        for i in range(self.obs_history.maxlen):
+            self.obs_history[i][env_ids] *= 0
+        for i in range(self.privileged_obs_history.maxlen):
+            self.privileged_obs_history[i][env_ids] *= 0
+
+        self.rand_torque_delay[env_ids] = torch.randint(
+            0, self.torque_deque_size, (len(env_ids),), dtype=torch.int32, device=self.device
+        )
+        self.torque_deque[:, env_ids].zero_()
+
+        self.rand_leg_linear_dof_pos_offset[env_ids, :][:, self.leg_linear_dof_indices] = (
+            torch_rand_float(
+                -1.0,
+                1.0,
+                (len(env_ids), len(self.leg_linear_dof_indices)),
+                device=self.device,
+            )
+            * self.leg_linear_dof_pos_offset_max
+        )
+
+        self.reset_base_vel_history(env_ids)
+        self.reset_z_pos_history(env_ids)
+
+        self.sim_step_counter[env_ids] = 0
+
+        self.arm_pos_command_generators.update_random_params(env_ids, self.cfg.domain_rand.randomize_arm_motion)
+        self.arm_pos_command_generators_in_walk.update_random_params(env_ids, self.cfg.domain_rand.randomize_arm_motion)
+
+    def reset_base_vel_history(self, env_ids):
+        self.base_vel_history[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.base_vel_history_size[env_ids] = 0
+
+    def reset_z_pos_history(self, env_ids):
+        self.z_pos_history[env_ids] = 0.0
+        self.z_pos_history_size[env_ids] = 0
+
+    def make_robot_data(self, actions: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None):
+        """Create a RobotData object from the current environment.
+
+        Args:
+            actions: 1-D tensor with shape (env.num_dofs), computed from the policy given the CURRENT env obs.
+
+        Returns:
+            R01RobotData: A RobotData object representing the current environment.
+        """
+        from humanoid.envs.r01_amp.r01_robot_data import R01RobotData
+
+        return R01RobotData(self.gym.get_sim_time(self.sim), self, actions)
+
+    def _reset_dofs_amp(self, env_ids, frames):
+        """Resets DOF position and velocities of selected environmments
+        Positions are randomly selected within 0.5:1.5 x default positions.
+        Velocities are set to zero.
+
+        Args:
+            env_ids (List[int]): Environemnt ids
+            frames: AMP frames to initialize motion with
+        """
+        self.last_dof_pos[env_ids, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim] = self.amp_loader.get_joint_pos_batch(frames)
+        self.dof_pos[env_ids, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim] = self.amp_loader.get_joint_pos_batch(frames)
+        self.dof_vel[env_ids, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim] = self.amp_loader.get_joint_vel_batch(frames)
+        if self.cfg.domain_rand.dof_vel_perturbation:
+            self.dof_vel[env_ids, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim] += (
+                torch_rand_float(-1.0, 1.0, (len(env_ids), self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim), device=self.device)
+                * self.cfg.domain_rand.dof_vel_perturbation_max
+            )
+
+        if self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim < self.num_dof:
+            self.dof_pos[env_ids, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :] = self.default_dof_pos.squeeze(0)[
+                self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :
+            ] * torch_rand_float(
+                0.5, 1.5, (len(env_ids), self.num_dof - self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim), device=self.device
+            ) + torch_rand_float(
+                -0.1, 0.1, (len(env_ids), self.num_dof - self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim), device=self.device
+            )
+            self.dof_vel[env_ids, self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim :] = 0.0
+
+        env_ids_int32 = env_ids.to(dtype=torch.int32)
+        self.gym.set_dof_state_tensor_indexed(
+            self.sim, gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(self.dof_state), gymtorch.unwrap_tensor(env_ids_int32), len(env_ids_int32)
+        )
+
+    def get_amp_observations(self):
+        """
+        Returns the observations for the AMP environment
+
+        Returns:
+            torch.Tensor: The observations for the AMP environment
+        """
+
+        base_lin_vel = self.base_lin_vel
+        base_ang_vel = self.base_ang_vel
+        projected_gravity = self.projected_gravity
+        torso_projected_gravity = self.torso_projected_gravity
+        joint_pos = self.dof_pos
+        joint_vel = self.dof_vel
+        fp, fv = self.feet_pos, self.feet_vel
+        z_pos = self.root_states[:, 2:3]
+        return torch.cat(
+            (
+                # base_lin_vel,
+                # base_ang_vel,
+                fp,
+                # fv,
+                joint_pos[:, self.amp_obs_joint_indices],
+                # joint_pos[:, 0:12:6],  # hip yaw
+                # joint_pos[:, 1:12:6],  # hip pitch
+                # joint_pos[:, 2:12:6],  # hip roll
+                # joint_pos[:, 3:12:6],  # knee
+                # joint_pos[:, 4:12:6],  # ankle pitch
+                # joint_pos[:, 12:],  # waist and remaining joints (e.g. arms)
+                # joint_vel[:, 12:],  # waist and remaining joints (e.g. arms)
+                # joint_pos[:, 12:13],  # waist yaw
+                # joint_pos[:, 15:],  # remaining joints (e.g. arms)
+                # joint_vel[:, self.amp_obs_joint_indices],
+                # z_pos,
+                projected_gravity,
+                # torso_projected_gravity,
+            ),
+            dim=-1,
+        )
+
+    def _resample_commands(self, env_ids):
+        """
+        Randomly select commands of some environments.
+        (with certain chance of selecting the stop commands for each robot)
+        This function will override the same function name under legged_robot.py
+
+        Args:
+            env_ids (List[int]): Environments ids for which new commands are needed
+        """
+        super()._resample_commands(env_ids)
+
+        # resample z_pos command
+        self.commands[env_ids, 4] = torch_rand_float(
+            self.command_ranges["z_pos"][0],
+            self.command_ranges["z_pos"][1],
+            (len(env_ids), 1),
+            device=self.device,
+        ).squeeze(1)
+
+        # resample waist position
+        for i in range(3):
+            self.commands[env_ids, i + 5] = torch_rand_float(
+                self.command_ranges["waist_yrp"][i][0],
+                self.command_ranges["waist_yrp"][i][1],
+                (len(env_ids), 1),
+                device=self.device,
+            ).squeeze(1)
+
+        stop_command_prob = self.cfg.commands.stop_command_prob
+        stop_command_prob = min(1.0, max(0.0, stop_command_prob))
+        # for each robot, randomly decide if the command should be zero based on the stop_command_prob
+        if (stop_command_prob > 0.0) and (env_ids.shape[0] > 0):
+            apply_stop_command = torch.rand(len(env_ids), device=self.device) < stop_command_prob
+            self.commands[env_ids[apply_stop_command], :4] = 0.0
+
+        self.reset_base_vel_history(env_ids)
+        self.reset_z_pos_history(env_ids)
+
+        if not self.cfg.env.play_mode:
+            mode_roulette = torch_rand_float(0.0, 1.0, (len(env_ids), 1), device=self.device)
+            env_is_walking = torch.any(mode_roulette >= self.cfg.commands.stand_prob, dim=1)
+            walk_env_ids = env_ids[env_is_walking.nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()]
+            stand_env_ids = env_ids[(env_is_walking == 0).nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()]
+            # for walking envs, z_pos command set to 1.0
+            self.commands[walk_env_ids, 4] = 1.0
+            self.commands[walk_env_ids, 5] *= 1.0
+            self.commands[walk_env_ids, 6] *= 0.5
+            self.commands[walk_env_ids, 7] *= 0.5
+            # for standing envs, all vel commands set to 0.0
+            self.commands[stand_env_ids, :4] = 0.0
+
+    # ================================================ Rewards ================================================== #
+
+    def _reward_torques(self):
+        # Penalize torques
+        return torch.sum(torch.square(self.torques[:, : self.num_actions]), dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_torques_percent(self):
+        return torch.sum(torch.square((self.torques / self.torque_limits)[:, : self.num_actions]), dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_dof_vel(self):
+        # Penalize dof velocities
+        return torch.sum(torch.square(self.dof_vel[:, : self.num_actions]), dim=1)
+
+    # def _reward_feet_vel(self):
+    #     # Penalize feet velocities
+    #     return torch.sum(torch.square(self.feet_vel), dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_feet_vel_world(self):
+        # Penalize feet velocities [x, y, z, rx, ry, rz] in world frame
+        return torch.sum(torch.square(self.rigid_state[:, self.feet_indices, 7:13]), dim=(2, 1))
+
+    def _reward_feet_ground_alignment(self):
+        # get rotation matrix of feet from rigit_state's quat
+        feet_quat = self.rigid_state[:, self.feet_indices, 3:7]
+        # get roll and pitch of feet from quat
+        rpy = torch.zeros((self.num_envs, len(self.feet_indices), 3), device=self.device)
+        for i in range(len(self.feet_indices)):
+            rpy[:, i, :] = get_euler_xyz_tensor(feet_quat[:, i, :])
+        # penalize roll and pitch
+        return torch.sum(torch.square(rpy[:, :, 0]), dim=1) + torch.sum(torch.square(rpy[:, :, 1]), dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_dof_acc(self):
+        # Penalize dof accelerations
+        return torch.sum(
+            torch.square((self.last_dof_vel[:, : self.num_actions] - self.dof_vel[:, : self.num_actions]) / self.dt),
+            dim=1,
+        )
+
+    def _reward_dof_pos_limits(self):
+        # Penalize dof positions too close to the limit
+        out_of_limits = -(self.dof_pos - self.soft_dof_pos_limits[:, 0]).clip(max=0.0)[
+            :, : self.num_actions
+        ]  # lower limit
+        out_of_limits += (self.dof_pos - self.soft_dof_pos_limits[:, 1]).clip(min=0.0)[
+            :, : self.num_actions
+        ]  # upper limit
+        return torch.sum(out_of_limits[:, : self.num_actions], dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_dof_vel_limits(self):
+        # Penalize dof velocities too close to the limit
+        # clip to max error = 1 rad/s per joint to avoid huge penalties
+        return torch.sum(
+            ((torch.abs(self.dof_vel) - self.soft_dof_vel_limits).clip(min=0.0))[:, : self.num_actions],
+            dim=1,
+        )
+
+    def _reward_torque_limits(self):
+        # penalize torques too close to the limit
+        return torch.sum(
+            ((torch.abs(self.torques) - self.soft_torque_limits).clip(min=0.0))[:, : self.num_actions],
+            dim=1,
+        )
+
+    def _reward_tracking_z_pos(self):
+        # Tracking of z pos commands
+        z_pos_error = torch.square(self.commands[:, 4] - self.root_states[:, 2])
+
+        is_env_walking = torch.any(torch.norm(self.commands[:, :3], dim=1).unsqueeze(-1) > 0.2, dim=1)
+        walk_env_ids = is_env_walking.nonzero(as_tuple=False).flatten()
+        avg_z_pos_error = torch.square(self.commands[:, 4] - self.avg_z_pos)
+        rew_term = torch.exp(-z_pos_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_z_pos)
+        rew_term[walk_env_ids] = torch.exp(-avg_z_pos_error[walk_env_ids] / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_z_pos)
+
+        return rew_term
+
+    def _reward_tracking_avg_lin_vel(self):
+        # Tracking of linear velocity commands (xy axes)
+        lin_vel_error = torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, :2] - self.base_avg_vel[:, :2]), dim=1)
+        return torch.exp(-lin_vel_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_lin_vel)
+
+    def _reward_tracking_avg_ang_vel(self):
+        # Tracking of angular velocity commands (yaw)
+        ang_vel_error = torch.square(self.commands[:, 2] - self.base_avg_vel[:, 2])
+        return torch.exp(-ang_vel_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_ang_vel)
+
+    def _reward_tracking_lin_vel(self):
+        # Tracking of linear velocity commands (xy axes)
+        lin_vel_error = torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, :2] - self.base_lin_vel[:, :2]), dim=1)
+        rew_term = torch.exp(-lin_vel_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_lin_vel)
+        return rew_term
+
+    def _reward_tracking_ang_vel(self):
+        # Tracking of angular velocity commands (yaw)
+        ang_vel_error = torch.square(self.commands[:, 2] - self.base_ang_vel[:, 2])
+        rew_term = torch.exp(-ang_vel_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_ang_vel)
+        return rew_term
+
+    def _reward_tracking_waist_yrp(self):
+        # Tracking of waist rpy commands
+        waist_yrp_error = torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, 5:] - self.dof_pos[:, 12:15]), dim=1)
+        return torch.exp(-waist_yrp_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_waist)
+        # return torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, 5:] - self.dof_pos[:, 12:15]), dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_stand_still(self):
+        # Penalize motion at zero commands
+        return torch.sum(
+            (torch.abs(self.dof_pos - self.standing_dof_pos))[:, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim], dim=1
+        ) * (torch.norm(self.commands[:, :3], dim=1) < 0.1)
+
+    def _reward_default_joint_pos(self):
+        """
+        Calculates the reward for keeping joint positions close to default positions, with a focus
+        on penalizing deviation in yaw and roll directions. Excludes yaw and roll from the main penalty.
+        """
+        joint_diff = (self.dof_pos - self.default_dof_pos)[:, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim]
+        left_yaw_roll = joint_diff.index_select(1, torch.tensor([0, 2], device=self.device))
+        right_yaw_roll = joint_diff.index_select(1, torch.tensor([6, 8], device=self.device))
+        yaw_roll = torch.norm(left_yaw_roll, dim=1) + torch.norm(right_yaw_roll, dim=1)
+        yaw_roll = torch.clamp(yaw_roll - 0.1, 0, 50)
+        return torch.exp(-yaw_roll * 100)  # - 0.01 * torch.norm(joint_diff, dim=1)
+
+    def _reward_energy(self):
+        return torch.sum(
+            torch.abs(
+                torch.multiply(
+                    self.torques[:, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim],
+                    self.dof_vel[:, : self.cfg.env.amp_motion_dof_dim],
+                )
+            ),
+            dim=1,
+        )
+
+    def _reward_pelvis_ground_alignment(self):
+        # penalize roll and pitch
+        return torch.square(self.base_euler_xyz[:, 0]) + torch.square(self.base_euler_xyz[:, 1])
+
+    def _reward_tracking_torso_rp(self):
+        # Tracking of torso roll and pitch commands
+        rpy = get_euler_xyz_tensor(self.torso_quat)
+        rp_error = torch.sum(torch.square(self.commands[:, 6:] - rpy[:, :2]), dim=1)
+        return torch.exp(-rp_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_torso_rp)
+
+    def _reward_tracking_waist_yaw(self):
+        # Tracking of waist rpy commands
+        waist_yaw_error = torch.square(self.commands[:, 5] - self.dof_pos[:, 12])
+        return torch.exp(-waist_yaw_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_waist_yaw)
+        # return (self.dof_pos[:, 12] > self.waist_soft_limit[0, 0]) * (self.dof_pos[:, 12] < self.waist_soft_limit[0, 1]) * torch.exp(-waist_yaw_error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_waist_yaw)
+
+    def _reward_tracking_torso_ori(self):
+        # Tracking of torso orientation commands
+        command_quat = quat_from_euler_xyz(self.commands[:, 6], self.commands[:, 7], self.commands[:, 5])
+        error = torch.sum(torch.square(quat_error(self.torso_quat, command_quat)), dim=1)
+        return torch.exp(-error / self.cfg.rewards.tracking_sigma_torso_ori)
+
+    def _reward_waist_soft_limit(self):
+        # Penalize waist positions too close to the soft limits
+        out_of_limits = -(self.dof_pos[:, 12:15] - self.waist_soft_limit[:, 0]).clip(max=0.0)  # lower limit
+        out_of_limits += (self.dof_pos[:, 12:15] - self.waist_soft_limit[:, 1]).clip(min=0.0)  # upper limit
+        return torch.sum(torch.square(out_of_limits), dim=1)
+        # return torch.sum(out_of_limits[:, : self.num_actions], dim=1)

+from isaacgym import gymtorch, gymapi

+import torch

+            self.num_envs, dtype=torch.long, device=self.device, requires_grad=False

+        self.target_frame_dof_pos = torch.zeros(

+        )
+        self.target_frame_proj_gravity = self.gravity_vec.clone()
+        self.target_frame_torso_proj_g = self.gravity_vec.clone()
+        self.target_frame_root_h = torch.zeros(

+

+        )

+        )
+        self.hand_pos_dim = 6
+        self.hand_pos = torch.zeros(

+        )

+
